48 // This should get the default rounding mode from the kernel. We just set the ----
49 // default here, but this could change if the OpenCL rounding mode pragmas are ----
50 // used. ----
51 // ----
52 // The denormal mode here should match what is reported by the OpenCL runtime ----
53 // for the CL_FP_DENORM bit from CL_DEVICE_{HALF|SINGLE|DOUBLE}_FP_CONFIG, but ----
54 // can also be override to flush with the -cl-denorms-are-zero compiler flag. ----
55 // ----
56 // AMD OpenCL only sets flush none and reports CL_FP_DENORM for double ----
57 // precision, and leaves single precision to flush all and does not report ----
58 // CL_FP_DENORM for CL_DEVICE_SINGLE_FP_CONFIG. Mesa's OpenCL currently reports ----
59 // CL_FP_DENORM for both. ----
60 // ----
61 // FIXME: It seems some instructions do not support single precision denormals ----
62 // regardless of the mode (exp_*_f32, rcp_*_f32, rsq_*_f32, rsq_*f32, sqrt_f32, ----
63 // and sin_f32, cos_f32 on most parts). ----
64 ----
65 // We want to use these instructions, and using fp32 denormals also causes ----
66 // instructions to run at the double precision rate for the device so it's ----
67 // probably best to just report no single precision denormals. ----
68 static uint32_t getFPMode(SIModeRegisterDefaults Mode) { 0
69 return FP_ROUND_MODE_SP(FP_ROUND_ROUND_TO_NEAREST) | ----
70 FP_ROUND_MODE_DP(FP_ROUND_ROUND_TO_NEAREST) | ----
71 FP_DENORM_MODE_SP(Mode.fpDenormModeSPValue()) | 0
72 FP_DENORM_MODE_DP(Mode.fpDenormModeDPValue()); 0
73 } ----

165 bool AMDGPUAsmPrinter::isBlockOnlyReachableByFallthrough( 0
166 const MachineBasicBlock *MBB) const { ----
167 if (!AsmPrinter::isBlockOnlyReachableByFallthrough(MBB)) 0
168 return false; 0
169 ----
170 if (MBB->empty()) 0
171 return true; 0
172 ----
173 // If this is a block implementing a long branch, an expression relative to ----
174 // the start of the block is needed. to the start of the block. ----
175 // XXX - Is there a smarter way to check this? ----
176 return (MBB->back().getOpcode() != AMDGPU::S_SETPC_B64); 0
177 } ----

188 ----

190 // Make sure function's xnack settings are compatible with module's ----
191 // xnack settings. ----
192 if (FunctionTargetID.isXnackSupported() && 0
193 FunctionTargetID.getXnackSetting() != IsaInfo::TargetIDSetting::Any && 0

222 } ----

224 void AMDGPUAsmPrinter::emitFunctionBodyEnd() { 0
225 const SIMachineFunctionInfo &MFI = *MF->getInfo(); 0
226 if (!MFI.isEntryFunction()) 0
227 return; 0
228 ----
229 if (TM.getTargetTriple().getOS() != Triple::AMDHSA || 0

232 ----

236 auto &ReadOnlySection = *ObjectFileInfo.getReadOnlySection(); 0
237 ----
238 Streamer.pushSection(); 0
239 Streamer.switchSection(&ReadOnlySection); 0
240 ----
241 // CP microcode requires the kernel descriptor to be allocated on 64 byte ----

261 } 0

300 void AMDGPUAsmPrinter::emitGlobalVariable(const GlobalVariable *GV) { 0
301 if (GV->getAddressSpace() == AMDGPUAS::LOCAL_ADDRESS) { 0
302 if (GV->hasInitializer() && !isa(GV->getInitializer())) { 0
303 OutContext.reportError({}, 0
304 Twine(GV->getName()) + 0
305 ": unsupported initializer for address space"); 0
306 return; 0
307 } ----
308 ----
309 // LDS variables aren't emitted in HSA or PAL yet. ----
310 const Triple::OSType OS = TM.getTargetTriple().getOS(); 0
311 if (OS == Triple::AMDHSA || OS == Triple::AMDPAL) 0
312 return; 0
313 ----
314 MCSymbol *GVSym = getSymbol(GV); 0
315 ----
316 GVSym->redefineIfPossible(); 0
317 if (GVSym->isDefined() || GVSym->isVariable()) 0
318 report_fatal_error("symbol '" + Twine(GVSym->getName()) + 0
319 "' is already defined"); 0
320 ----
321 const DataLayout &DL = GV->getParent()->getDataLayout(); 0
322 uint64_t Size = DL.getTypeAllocSize(GV->getValueType()); 0
323 Align Alignment = GV->getAlign().value_or(Align(4)); 0
324 ----
325 emitVisibility(GVSym, GV->getVisibility(), !GV->isDeclaration()); 0
326 emitLinkage(GV, GVSym); 0
327 auto TS = getTargetStreamer(); 0
328 TS->emitAMDGPULDS(GVSym, Size, Alignment); 0
329 return; 0
330 } ----
331 ----
332 AsmPrinter::emitGlobalVariable(GV); 0
333 } ----

335 bool AMDGPUAsmPrinter::doInitialization(Module &M) { 0
336 CodeObjectVersion = AMDGPU::getCodeObjectVersion(M); 0
337 ----
338 if (TM.getTargetTriple().getOS() == Triple::AMDHSA) { 0
339 switch (CodeObjectVersion) { 0
340 case AMDGPU::AMDHSA_COV2: 0
341 HSAMetadataStream.reset(new HSAMD::MetadataStreamerYamlV2()); 0
342 break; 0
343 case AMDGPU::AMDHSA_COV3: 0
344 HSAMetadataStream.reset(new HSAMD::MetadataStreamerMsgPackV3()); 0
345 break; 0
346 case AMDGPU::AMDHSA_COV4: 0
347 HSAMetadataStream.reset(new HSAMD::MetadataStreamerMsgPackV4()); 0
348 break; 0
349 case AMDGPU::AMDHSA_COV5: 0
350 HSAMetadataStream.reset(new HSAMD::MetadataStreamerMsgPackV5()); 0
351 break; 0
352 default: 0
353 report_fatal_error("Unexpected code object version"); 0
354 } ----
355 } ----
356 return AsmPrinter::doInitialization(M); 0
357 } ----

359 bool AMDGPUAsmPrinter::doFinalization(Module &M) { 0
360 // Pad with s_code_end to help tools and guard against instruction prefetch ----
361 // causing stale data in caches. Arguably this should be done by the linker, ----
362 // which is why this isn't done for Mesa. ----
363 const MCSubtargetInfo &STI = *getGlobalSTI(); 0
364 if ((AMDGPU::isGFX10Plus(STI) || AMDGPU::isGFX90A(STI)) && 0
365 (STI.getTargetTriple().getOS() == Triple::AMDHSA || 0
366 STI.getTargetTriple().getOS() == Triple::AMDPAL)) { 0
367 OutStreamer->switchSection(getObjFileLowering().getTextSection()); 0
368 getTargetStreamer()->EmitCodeEnd(STI); 0
369 } ----
370 ----
371 return AsmPrinter::doFinalization(M); 0
372 } ----

392 uint16_t AMDGPUAsmPrinter::getAmdhsaKernelCodeProperties( 0
393 const MachineFunction &MF) const { ----
394 const SIMachineFunctionInfo &MFI = *MF.getInfo(); 0
395 uint16_t KernelCodeProperties = 0; 0
396 ----
397 if (MFI.hasPrivateSegmentBuffer()) { 0
398 KernelCodeProperties |= 0
399 amdhsa::KERNEL_CODE_PROPERTY_ENABLE_SGPR_PRIVATE_SEGMENT_BUFFER; ----
400 } ----
401 if (MFI.hasDispatchPtr()) { 0
402 KernelCodeProperties |= 0
403 amdhsa::KERNEL_CODE_PROPERTY_ENABLE_SGPR_DISPATCH_PTR; ----
404 } ----
405 if (MFI.hasQueuePtr() && CodeObjectVersion < AMDGPU::AMDHSA_COV5) { 0
406 KernelCodeProperties |= 0
407 amdhsa::KERNEL_CODE_PROPERTY_ENABLE_SGPR_QUEUE_PTR; ----
408 } ----
409 if (MFI.hasKernargSegmentPtr()) { 0
410 KernelCodeProperties |= 0
411 amdhsa::KERNEL_CODE_PROPERTY_ENABLE_SGPR_KERNARG_SEGMENT_PTR; ----
412 } ----
413 if (MFI.hasDispatchID()) { 0
414 KernelCodeProperties |= 0
415 amdhsa::KERNEL_CODE_PROPERTY_ENABLE_SGPR_DISPATCH_ID; ----
416 } ----
417 if (MFI.hasFlatScratchInit()) { 0
418 KernelCodeProperties |= 0
419 amdhsa::KERNEL_CODE_PROPERTY_ENABLE_SGPR_FLAT_SCRATCH_INIT; ----
420 } ----
421 if (MF.getSubtarget().isWave32()) { 0
422 KernelCodeProperties |= 0
423 amdhsa::KERNEL_CODE_PROPERTY_ENABLE_WAVEFRONT_SIZE32; ----
424 } ----
425 ----
426 if (CurrentProgramInfo.DynamicCallStack && 0
427 CodeObjectVersion >= AMDGPU::AMDHSA_COV5) 0
428 KernelCodeProperties |= amdhsa::KERNEL_CODE_PROPERTY_USES_DYNAMIC_STACK; 0
429 ----
430 return KernelCodeProperties; 0
431 } ----

433 amdhsa::kernel_descriptor_t AMDGPUAsmPrinter::getAmdhsaKernelDescriptor( 0
434 const MachineFunction &MF, ----
435 const SIProgramInfo &PI) const { ----
436 const GCNSubtarget &STM = MF.getSubtarget(); 0
437 const Function &F = MF.getFunction(); 0
438 ----
439 amdhsa::kernel_descriptor_t KernelDescriptor; ----
440 memset(&KernelDescriptor, 0x0, sizeof(KernelDescriptor)); 0
441 ----
442 assert(isUInt<32>(PI.ScratchSize)); 0
443 assert(isUInt<32>(PI.getComputePGMRSrc1())); 0
444 assert(isUInt<32>(PI.getComputePGMRSrc2())); 0
445 ----
446 KernelDescriptor.group_segment_fixed_size = PI.LDSSize; 0
447 KernelDescriptor.private_segment_fixed_size = PI.ScratchSize; 0
448 ----
449 Align MaxKernArgAlign; 0
450 KernelDescriptor.kernarg_size = STM.getKernArgSegmentSize(F, MaxKernArgAlign); 0
451 ----
452 KernelDescriptor.compute_pgm_rsrc1 = PI.getComputePGMRSrc1(); 0
453 KernelDescriptor.compute_pgm_rsrc2 = PI.getComputePGMRSrc2(); 0
454 KernelDescriptor.kernel_code_properties = getAmdhsaKernelCodeProperties(MF); 0
455 ----
456 assert(STM.hasGFX90AInsts() || CurrentProgramInfo.ComputePGMRSrc3GFX90A == 0); 0
457 if (STM.hasGFX90AInsts()) 0
458 KernelDescriptor.compute_pgm_rsrc3 = 0
459 CurrentProgramInfo.ComputePGMRSrc3GFX90A; 0
460 ----
461 return KernelDescriptor; 0
462 } ----

464 bool AMDGPUAsmPrinter::runOnMachineFunction(MachineFunction &MF) { 0
465 // Init target streamer lazily on the first function so that previous passes ----
466 // can set metadata. ----
467 if (!IsTargetStreamerInitialized) 0
468 initTargetStreamer(*MF.getFunction().getParent()); 0
469 ----
470 ResourceUsage = &getAnalysis(); 0
471 CurrentProgramInfo = SIProgramInfo(); 0
472 ----
473 const AMDGPUMachineFunction *MFI = MF.getInfo(); 0
474 ----
475 // The starting address of all shader programs must be 256 bytes aligned. ----
476 // Regular functions just need the basic required instruction alignment. ----
477 MF.setAlignment(MFI->isEntryFunction() ? Align(256) : Align(4)); 0
478 ----
479 SetupMachineFunction(MF); 0
480 ----
481 const GCNSubtarget &STM = MF.getSubtarget(); 0
482 MCContext &Context = getObjFileLowering().getContext(); 0
483 // FIXME: This should be an explicit check for Mesa. ----
484 if (!STM.isAmdHsaOS() && !STM.isAmdPalOS()) { 0
485 MCSectionELF *ConfigSection = ----
486 Context.getELFSection(".AMDGPU.config", ELF::SHT_PROGBITS, 0); 0
487 OutStreamer->switchSection(ConfigSection); 0
488 } ----
489 ----
490 if (MFI->isModuleEntryFunction()) { 0
491 getSIProgramInfo(CurrentProgramInfo, MF); 0
492 } ----
493 ----
494 if (STM.isAmdPalOS()) { 0
495 if (MFI->isEntryFunction()) 0
496 EmitPALMetadata(MF, CurrentProgramInfo); 0
497 else if (MFI->isModuleEntryFunction()) 0
498 emitPALFunctionMetadata(MF); 0
499 } else if (!STM.isAmdHsaOS()) { 0
500 EmitProgramInfoSI(MF, CurrentProgramInfo); 0
501 } ----
502 ----
503 DumpCodeInstEmitter = nullptr; 0
504 if (STM.dumpCode()) { 0
505 // For -dumpcode, get the assembler out of the streamer, even if it does ----
506 // not really want to let us have it. This only works with -filetype=obj. ----
507 bool SaveFlag = OutStreamer->getUseAssemblerInfoForParsing(); 0
508 OutStreamer->setUseAssemblerInfoForParsing(true); 0
509 MCAssembler *Assembler = OutStreamer->getAssemblerPtr(); 0
510 OutStreamer->setUseAssemblerInfoForParsing(SaveFlag); 0
511 if (Assembler) 0
512 DumpCodeInstEmitter = Assembler->getEmitterPtr(); 0
513 } ----
514 ----
515 DisasmLines.clear(); 0
516 HexLines.clear(); 0
517 DisasmLineMaxLen = 0; 0
518 ----
519 emitFunctionBody(); 0
520 ----
521 emitResourceUsageRemarks(MF, CurrentProgramInfo, MFI->isModuleEntryFunction(), 0
522 STM.hasMAIInsts()); 0
523 ----
524 if (isVerbose()) { 0
525 MCSectionELF *CommentSection = ----
526 Context.getELFSection(".AMDGPU.csdata", ELF::SHT_PROGBITS, 0); 0
527 OutStreamer->switchSection(CommentSection); 0
528 ----
529 if (!MFI->isEntryFunction()) { 0
530 OutStreamer->emitRawComment(" Function info:", false); 0
531 const AMDGPUResourceUsageAnalysis::SIFunctionResourceInfo &Info = ----
532 ResourceUsage->getResourceInfo(&MF.getFunction()); 0
533 emitCommonFunctionComments( 0
534 Info.NumVGPR, 0
535 STM.hasMAIInsts() ? Info.NumAGPR : std::optional(), 0
536 Info.getTotalNumVGPRs(STM), 0
537 Info.getTotalNumSGPRs(MF.getSubtarget()), 0
538 Info.PrivateSegmentSize, getFunctionCodeSize(MF), MFI); 0
539 return false; 0
540 } ----
541 ----
542 OutStreamer->emitRawComment(" Kernel info:", false); 0
543 emitCommonFunctionComments( 0
544 CurrentProgramInfo.NumArchVGPR, ----
545 STM.hasMAIInsts() ? CurrentProgramInfo.NumAccVGPR 0
546 : std::optional(), ----
547 CurrentProgramInfo.NumVGPR, CurrentProgramInfo.NumSGPR, ----
548 CurrentProgramInfo.ScratchSize, getFunctionCodeSize(MF), MFI); ----
549 ----
550 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
551 " FloatMode: " + Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.FloatMode), false); 0
552 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
553 " IeeeMode: " + Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.IEEEMode), false); 0
554 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
555 " LDSByteSize: " + Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.LDSSize) + 0
556 " bytes/workgroup (compile time only)", false); 0
557 ----
558 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
559 " SGPRBlocks: " + Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.SGPRBlocks), false); 0
560 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
561 " VGPRBlocks: " + Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.VGPRBlocks), false); 0
562 ----
563 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
564 " NumSGPRsForWavesPerEU: " + 0
565 Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.NumSGPRsForWavesPerEU), false); 0
566 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
567 " NumVGPRsForWavesPerEU: " + 0
568 Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.NumVGPRsForWavesPerEU), false); 0
569 ----
570 if (STM.hasGFX90AInsts()) 0
571 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
572 " AccumOffset: " + 0
573 Twine((CurrentProgramInfo.AccumOffset + 1) * 4), false); 0
574 ----
575 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
576 " Occupancy: " + 0
577 Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.Occupancy), false); 0
578 ----
579 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
580 " WaveLimiterHint : " + Twine(MFI->needsWaveLimiter()), false); 0
581 ----
582 OutStreamer->emitRawComment(" COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC2:SCRATCH_EN: " + 0
583 Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.ScratchEnable), 0
584 false); ----
585 OutStreamer->emitRawComment(" COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC2:USER_SGPR: " + 0
586 Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.UserSGPR), 0
587 false); ----
588 OutStreamer->emitRawComment(" COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC2:TRAP_HANDLER: " + 0
589 Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.TrapHandlerEnable), 0
590 false); ----
591 OutStreamer->emitRawComment(" COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC2:TGID_X_EN: " + 0
592 Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.TGIdXEnable), 0
593 false); ----
594 OutStreamer->emitRawComment(" COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC2:TGID_Y_EN: " + 0
595 Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.TGIdYEnable), 0
596 false); ----
597 OutStreamer->emitRawComment(" COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC2:TGID_Z_EN: " + 0
598 Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.TGIdZEnable), 0
599 false); ----
600 OutStreamer->emitRawComment(" COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC2:TIDIG_COMP_CNT: " + 0
601 Twine(CurrentProgramInfo.TIdIGCompCount), 0
602 false); ----
603 ----
604 assert(STM.hasGFX90AInsts() || 0
605 CurrentProgramInfo.ComputePGMRSrc3GFX90A == 0); ----
606 if (STM.hasGFX90AInsts()) { 0
607 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
608 " COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC3_GFX90A:ACCUM_OFFSET: " + 0
609 Twine((AMDHSA_BITS_GET(CurrentProgramInfo.ComputePGMRSrc3GFX90A, 0
610 amdhsa::COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC3_GFX90A_ACCUM_OFFSET))), 0
611 false); ----
612 OutStreamer->emitRawComment( 0
613 " COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC3_GFX90A:TG_SPLIT: " + 0
614 Twine((AMDHSA_BITS_GET(CurrentProgramInfo.ComputePGMRSrc3GFX90A, 0
615 amdhsa::COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC3_GFX90A_TG_SPLIT))), 0
616 false); ----
617 } ----
618 } ----
619 ----
620 if (DumpCodeInstEmitter) { 0
621 ----
622 OutStreamer->switchSection( 0
623 Context.getELFSection(".AMDGPU.disasm", ELF::SHT_PROGBITS, 0)); 0
624 ----
625 for (size_t i = 0; i < DisasmLines.size(); ++i) { 0
626 std::string Comment = "\n"; 0
627 if (!HexLines[i].empty()) { 0
628 Comment = std::string(DisasmLineMaxLen - DisasmLines[i].size(), ' '); 0
629 Comment += " ; " + HexLines[i] + "\n"; 0
630 } ----
631 ----
632 OutStreamer->emitBytes(StringRef(DisasmLines[i])); 0
633 OutStreamer->emitBytes(StringRef(Comment)); 0
634 } 0
635 } ----
636 ----
637 return false; 0
638 } ----
639 ----
640 // TODO: Fold this into emitFunctionBodyStart. ----
641 void AMDGPUAsmPrinter::initializeTargetID(const Module &M) { 0
642 // In the beginning all features are either 'Any' or 'NotSupported', ----
643 // depending on global target features. This will cover empty modules. ----
644 getTargetStreamer()->initializeTargetID( 0
645 *getGlobalSTI(), getGlobalSTI()->getFeatureString(), CodeObjectVersion); 0
646 ----
647 // If module is empty, we are done. ----
648 if (M.empty()) 0
649 return; 0
650 ----
651 // If module is not empty, need to find first 'Off' or 'On' feature ----
652 // setting per feature from functions in module. ----
653 for (auto &F : M) { 0
654 auto &TSTargetID = getTargetStreamer()->getTargetID(); 0
655 if ((!TSTargetID->isXnackSupported() || TSTargetID->isXnackOnOrOff()) && 0
656 (!TSTargetID->isSramEccSupported() || TSTargetID->isSramEccOnOrOff())) 0
657 break; 0
658 ----
659 const GCNSubtarget &STM = TM.getSubtarget(F); 0
660 const IsaInfo::AMDGPUTargetID &STMTargetID = STM.getTargetID(); 0
661 if (TSTargetID->isXnackSupported()) 0
662 if (TSTargetID->getXnackSetting() == IsaInfo::TargetIDSetting::Any) 0
663 TSTargetID->setXnackSetting(STMTargetID.getXnackSetting()); 0
664 if (TSTargetID->isSramEccSupported()) 0
665 if (TSTargetID->getSramEccSetting() == IsaInfo::TargetIDSetting::Any) 0
666 TSTargetID->setSramEccSetting(STMTargetID.getSramEccSetting()); 0
667 } ----
668 } ----
669 ----
670 uint64_t AMDGPUAsmPrinter::getFunctionCodeSize(const MachineFunction &MF) const { 0
671 const GCNSubtarget &STM = MF.getSubtarget(); 0
672 const SIInstrInfo *TII = STM.getInstrInfo(); 0
673 ----
674 uint64_t CodeSize = 0; 0
675 ----
676 for (const MachineBasicBlock &MBB : MF) { 0
677 for (const MachineInstr &MI : MBB) { 0
678 // TODO: CodeSize should account for multiple functions. ----
679 ----
680 // TODO: Should we count size of debug info? ----
681 if (MI.isDebugInstr()) 0
682 continue; 0
683 ----
684 CodeSize += TII->getInstSizeInBytes(MI); 0
685 } ----
686 } ----
687 ----
688 return CodeSize; 0
689 } ----
690 ----
691 void AMDGPUAsmPrinter::getSIProgramInfo(SIProgramInfo &ProgInfo, 0
692 const MachineFunction &MF) { ----
693 const AMDGPUResourceUsageAnalysis::SIFunctionResourceInfo &Info = ----
694 ResourceUsage->getResourceInfo(&MF.getFunction()); 0
695 const GCNSubtarget &STM = MF.getSubtarget(); 0
696 ----
697 ProgInfo.NumArchVGPR = Info.NumVGPR; 0
698 ProgInfo.NumAccVGPR = Info.NumAGPR; 0
699 ProgInfo.NumVGPR = Info.getTotalNumVGPRs(STM); 0
700 ProgInfo.AccumOffset = alignTo(std::max(1, Info.NumVGPR), 4) / 4 - 1; 0
701 ProgInfo.TgSplit = STM.isTgSplitEnabled(); 0
702 ProgInfo.NumSGPR = Info.NumExplicitSGPR; 0
703 ProgInfo.ScratchSize = Info.PrivateSegmentSize; 0
704 ProgInfo.VCCUsed = Info.UsesVCC; 0
705 ProgInfo.FlatUsed = Info.UsesFlatScratch; 0
706 ProgInfo.DynamicCallStack = Info.HasDynamicallySizedStack || Info.HasRecursion; 0
707 ----
708 const uint64_t MaxScratchPerWorkitem = ----
709 STM.getMaxWaveScratchSize() / STM.getWavefrontSize(); 0
710 if (ProgInfo.ScratchSize > MaxScratchPerWorkitem) { 0
711 DiagnosticInfoStackSize DiagStackSize(MF.getFunction(), ----
712 ProgInfo.ScratchSize, ----
713 MaxScratchPerWorkitem, DS_Error); 0
714 MF.getFunction().getContext().diagnose(DiagStackSize); 0
715 } 0
716 ----
717 const SIMachineFunctionInfo *MFI = MF.getInfo(); 0
718 ----
719 // The calculations related to SGPR/VGPR blocks are ----
720 // duplicated in part in AMDGPUAsmParser::calculateGPRBlocks, and could be ----
721 // unified. ----
722 unsigned ExtraSGPRs = IsaInfo::getNumExtraSGPRs( 0
723 &STM, ProgInfo.VCCUsed, ProgInfo.FlatUsed, 0
724 getTargetStreamer()->getTargetID()->isXnackOnOrAny()); 0
725 ----
726 // Check the addressable register limit before we add ExtraSGPRs. ----
727 if (STM.getGeneration() >= AMDGPUSubtarget::VOLCANIC_ISLANDS && 0
728 !STM.hasSGPRInitBug()) { 0
729 unsigned MaxAddressableNumSGPRs = STM.getAddressableNumSGPRs(); 0
730 if (ProgInfo.NumSGPR > MaxAddressableNumSGPRs) { 0
731 // This can happen due to a compiler bug or when using inline asm. ----
732 LLVMContext &Ctx = MF.getFunction().getContext(); 0
733 DiagnosticInfoResourceLimit Diag( ----
734 MF.getFunction(), "addressable scalar registers", ProgInfo.NumSGPR, 0
735 MaxAddressableNumSGPRs, DS_Error, DK_ResourceLimit); 0
736 Ctx.diagnose(Diag); 0
737 ProgInfo.NumSGPR = MaxAddressableNumSGPRs - 1; 0
738 } 0
739 } ----
740 ----
741 // Account for extra SGPRs and VGPRs reserved for debugger use. ----
742 ProgInfo.NumSGPR += ExtraSGPRs; 0
743 ----
744 const Function &F = MF.getFunction(); 0
745 ----
746 // Ensure there are enough SGPRs and VGPRs for wave dispatch, where wave ----
747 // dispatch registers are function args. ----
748 unsigned WaveDispatchNumSGPR = 0, WaveDispatchNumVGPR = 0; 0
749 ----
750 if (isShader(F.getCallingConv())) { 0
751 bool IsPixelShader = ----
752 F.getCallingConv() == CallingConv::AMDGPU_PS && !STM.isAmdHsaOS(); 0
753 ----
754 // Calculate the number of VGPR registers based on the SPI input registers ----
755 uint32_t InputEna = 0; 0
756 uint32_t InputAddr = 0; 0
757 unsigned LastEna = 0; 0
758 ----
759 if (IsPixelShader) { 0
760 // Note for IsPixelShader: ----
761 // By this stage, all enabled inputs are tagged in InputAddr as well. ----
762 // We will use InputAddr to determine whether the input counts against the ----
763 // vgpr total and only use the InputEnable to determine the last input ----
764 // that is relevant - if extra arguments are used, then we have to honour ----
765 // the InputAddr for any intermediate non-enabled inputs. ----
766 InputEna = MFI->getPSInputEnable(); 0
767 InputAddr = MFI->getPSInputAddr(); 0
768 ----
769 // We only need to consider input args up to the last used arg. ----
770 assert((InputEna || InputAddr) && 0
771 "PSInputAddr and PSInputEnable should " ----
772 "never both be 0 for AMDGPU_PS shaders"); ----
773 // There are some rare circumstances where InputAddr is non-zero and ----
774 // InputEna can be set to 0. In this case we default to setting LastEna ----
775 // to 1. ----
776 LastEna = InputEna ? llvm::Log2_32(InputEna) + 1 : 1; 0
777 } ----
778 ----
779 // FIXME: We should be using the number of registers determined during ----
780 // calling convention lowering to legalize the types. ----
781 const DataLayout &DL = F.getParent()->getDataLayout(); 0
782 unsigned PSArgCount = 0; 0
783 unsigned IntermediateVGPR = 0; 0
784 for (auto &Arg : F.args()) { 0
785 unsigned NumRegs = (DL.getTypeSizeInBits(Arg.getType()) + 31) / 32; 0
786 if (Arg.hasAttribute(Attribute::InReg)) { 0
787 WaveDispatchNumSGPR += NumRegs; 0
788 } else { ----
789 // If this is a PS shader and we're processing the PS Input args (first ----
790 // 16 VGPR), use the InputEna and InputAddr bits to define how many ----
791 // VGPRs are actually used. ----
792 // Any extra VGPR arguments are handled as normal arguments (and ----
793 // contribute to the VGPR count whether they're used or not). ----
794 if (IsPixelShader && PSArgCount < 16) { 0
795 if ((1 << PSArgCount) & InputAddr) { 0
796 if (PSArgCount < LastEna) 0
797 WaveDispatchNumVGPR += NumRegs; 0
798 else ----
799 IntermediateVGPR += NumRegs; 0
800 } ----
801 PSArgCount++; 0
802 } else { ----
803 // If there are extra arguments we have to include the allocation for ----
804 // the non-used (but enabled with InputAddr) input arguments ----
805 if (IntermediateVGPR) { 0
806 WaveDispatchNumVGPR += IntermediateVGPR; 0
807 IntermediateVGPR = 0; 0
808 } ----
809 WaveDispatchNumVGPR += NumRegs; 0
810 } ----
811 } ----
812 } ----
813 ProgInfo.NumSGPR = std::max(ProgInfo.NumSGPR, WaveDispatchNumSGPR); 0
814 ProgInfo.NumArchVGPR = std::max(ProgInfo.NumVGPR, WaveDispatchNumVGPR); 0
815 ProgInfo.NumVGPR = 0
816 Info.getTotalNumVGPRs(STM, Info.NumAGPR, ProgInfo.NumArchVGPR); 0
817 } ----
818 ----
819 // Adjust number of registers used to meet default/requested minimum/maximum ----
820 // number of waves per execution unit request. ----
821 ProgInfo.NumSGPRsForWavesPerEU = std::max( 0
822 std::max(ProgInfo.NumSGPR, 1u), STM.getMinNumSGPRs(MFI->getMaxWavesPerEU())); 0
823 ProgInfo.NumVGPRsForWavesPerEU = std::max( 0
824 std::max(ProgInfo.NumVGPR, 1u), STM.getMinNumVGPRs(MFI->getMaxWavesPerEU())); 0
825 ----
826 if (STM.getGeneration() <= AMDGPUSubtarget::SEA_ISLANDS || 0
827 STM.hasSGPRInitBug()) { 0
828 unsigned MaxAddressableNumSGPRs = STM.getAddressableNumSGPRs(); 0
829 if (ProgInfo.NumSGPR > MaxAddressableNumSGPRs) { 0
830 // This can happen due to a compiler bug or when using inline asm to use ----
831 // the registers which are usually reserved for vcc etc. ----
832 LLVMContext &Ctx = MF.getFunction().getContext(); 0
833 DiagnosticInfoResourceLimit Diag(MF.getFunction(), "scalar registers", ----
834 ProgInfo.NumSGPR, MaxAddressableNumSGPRs, 0
835 DS_Error, DK_ResourceLimit); 0
836 Ctx.diagnose(Diag); 0
837 ProgInfo.NumSGPR = MaxAddressableNumSGPRs; 0
838 ProgInfo.NumSGPRsForWavesPerEU = MaxAddressableNumSGPRs; 0
839 } 0
840 } ----
841 ----
842 if (STM.hasSGPRInitBug()) { 0
843 ProgInfo.NumSGPR = 0
844 AMDGPU::IsaInfo::FIXED_NUM_SGPRS_FOR_INIT_BUG; ----
845 ProgInfo.NumSGPRsForWavesPerEU = 0
846 AMDGPU::IsaInfo::FIXED_NUM_SGPRS_FOR_INIT_BUG; ----
847 } ----
848 ----
849 if (MFI->getNumUserSGPRs() > STM.getMaxNumUserSGPRs()) { 0
850 LLVMContext &Ctx = MF.getFunction().getContext(); 0
851 DiagnosticInfoResourceLimit Diag(MF.getFunction(), "user SGPRs", ----
852 MFI->getNumUserSGPRs(), 0
853 STM.getMaxNumUserSGPRs(), DS_Error); 0
854 Ctx.diagnose(Diag); 0
855 } 0
856 ----
857 if (MFI->getLDSSize() > 0
858 static_cast(STM.getAddressableLocalMemorySize())) { 0
859 LLVMContext &Ctx = MF.getFunction().getContext(); 0
860 DiagnosticInfoResourceLimit Diag( ----
861 MF.getFunction(), "local memory", MFI->getLDSSize(), 0
862 STM.getAddressableLocalMemorySize(), DS_Error); 0
863 Ctx.diagnose(Diag); 0
864 } 0
865 ----
866 ProgInfo.SGPRBlocks = IsaInfo::getNumSGPRBlocks( 0
867 &STM, ProgInfo.NumSGPRsForWavesPerEU); ----
868 ProgInfo.VGPRBlocks = IsaInfo::getNumVGPRBlocks( 0
869 &STM, ProgInfo.NumVGPRsForWavesPerEU); ----
870 ----
871 const SIModeRegisterDefaults Mode = MFI->getMode(); 0
872 ----
873 // Set the value to initialize FP_ROUND and FP_DENORM parts of the mode ----
874 // register. ----
875 ProgInfo.FloatMode = getFPMode(Mode); 0
876 ----
877 ProgInfo.IEEEMode = Mode.IEEE; 0
878 ----
879 // Make clamp modifier on NaN input returns 0. ----
880 ProgInfo.DX10Clamp = Mode.DX10Clamp; 0
881 ----
882 unsigned LDSAlignShift; ----
883 if (STM.getGeneration() < AMDGPUSubtarget::SEA_ISLANDS) { 0
884 // LDS is allocated in 64 dword blocks. ----
885 LDSAlignShift = 8; 0
886 } else { ----
887 // LDS is allocated in 128 dword blocks. ----
888 LDSAlignShift = 9; 0
889 } ----
890 ----
891 ProgInfo.SGPRSpill = MFI->getNumSpilledSGPRs(); 0
892 ProgInfo.VGPRSpill = MFI->getNumSpilledVGPRs(); 0
893 ----
894 ProgInfo.LDSSize = MFI->getLDSSize(); 0
895 ProgInfo.LDSBlocks = 0
896 alignTo(ProgInfo.LDSSize, 1ULL << LDSAlignShift) >> LDSAlignShift; 0
897 ----
898 // Scratch is allocated in 64-dword or 256-dword blocks. ----
899 unsigned ScratchAlignShift = ----
900 STM.getGeneration() >= AMDGPUSubtarget::GFX11 ? 8 : 10; 0
901 // We need to program the hardware with the amount of scratch memory that ----
902 // is used by the entire wave. ProgInfo.ScratchSize is the amount of ----
903 // scratch memory used per thread. ----
904 ProgInfo.ScratchBlocks = divideCeil( 0
905 ProgInfo.ScratchSize * STM.getWavefrontSize(), 1ULL << ScratchAlignShift); 0
906 ----
907 if (getIsaVersion(getGlobalSTI()->getCPU()).Major >= 10) { 0
908 ProgInfo.WgpMode = STM.isCuModeEnabled() ? 0 : 1; 0
909 ProgInfo.MemOrdered = 1; 0
910 } ----
911 ----
912 // 0 = X, 1 = XY, 2 = XYZ ----
913 unsigned TIDIGCompCnt = 0; 0
914 if (MFI->hasWorkItemIDZ()) 0
915 TIDIGCompCnt = 2; 0
916 else if (MFI->hasWorkItemIDY()) 0
917 TIDIGCompCnt = 1; 0
918 ----
919 // The private segment wave byte offset is the last of the system SGPRs. We ----
920 // initially assumed it was allocated, and may have used it. It shouldn't harm ----
921 // anything to disable it if we know the stack isn't used here. We may still ----
922 // have emitted code reading it to initialize scratch, but if that's unused ----
923 // reading garbage should be OK. ----
924 ProgInfo.ScratchEnable = 0
925 ProgInfo.ScratchBlocks > 0 || ProgInfo.DynamicCallStack; 0
926 ProgInfo.UserSGPR = MFI->getNumUserSGPRs(); 0
927 // For AMDHSA, TRAP_HANDLER must be zero, as it is populated by the CP. ----
928 ProgInfo.TrapHandlerEnable = 0
929 STM.isAmdHsaOS() ? 0 : STM.isTrapHandlerEnabled(); 0
930 ProgInfo.TGIdXEnable = MFI->hasWorkGroupIDX(); 0
931 ProgInfo.TGIdYEnable = MFI->hasWorkGroupIDY(); 0
932 ProgInfo.TGIdZEnable = MFI->hasWorkGroupIDZ(); 0
933 ProgInfo.TGSizeEnable = MFI->hasWorkGroupInfo(); 0
934 ProgInfo.TIdIGCompCount = TIDIGCompCnt; 0
935 ProgInfo.EXCPEnMSB = 0; 0
936 // For AMDHSA, LDS_SIZE must be zero, as it is populated by the CP. ----
937 ProgInfo.LdsSize = STM.isAmdHsaOS() ? 0 : ProgInfo.LDSBlocks; 0
938 ProgInfo.EXCPEnable = 0; 0
939 ----
940 if (STM.hasGFX90AInsts()) { 0
941 AMDHSA_BITS_SET(ProgInfo.ComputePGMRSrc3GFX90A, 0
942 amdhsa::COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC3_GFX90A_ACCUM_OFFSET, ----
943 ProgInfo.AccumOffset); ----
944 AMDHSA_BITS_SET(ProgInfo.ComputePGMRSrc3GFX90A, 0
945 amdhsa::COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC3_GFX90A_TG_SPLIT, ----
946 ProgInfo.TgSplit); ----
947 } ----
948 ----
949 ProgInfo.Occupancy = STM.computeOccupancy(MF.getFunction(), ProgInfo.LDSSize, 0
950 ProgInfo.NumSGPRsForWavesPerEU, ----
951 ProgInfo.NumVGPRsForWavesPerEU); ----
952 } 0
953 ----
954 static unsigned getRsrcReg(CallingConv::ID CallConv) { 0
955 switch (CallConv) { 0
956 default: [[fallthrough]]; 0
957 case CallingConv::AMDGPU_CS: return R_00B848_COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC1; 0
958 case CallingConv::AMDGPU_LS: return R_00B528_SPI_SHADER_PGM_RSRC1_LS; 0
959 case CallingConv::AMDGPU_HS: return R_00B428_SPI_SHADER_PGM_RSRC1_HS; 0
960 case CallingConv::AMDGPU_ES: return R_00B328_SPI_SHADER_PGM_RSRC1_ES; 0
961 case CallingConv::AMDGPU_GS: return R_00B228_SPI_SHADER_PGM_RSRC1_GS; 0
962 case CallingConv::AMDGPU_VS: return R_00B128_SPI_SHADER_PGM_RSRC1_VS; 0
963 case CallingConv::AMDGPU_PS: return R_00B028_SPI_SHADER_PGM_RSRC1_PS; 0
964 } ----
965 } ----
966 ----
967 void AMDGPUAsmPrinter::EmitProgramInfoSI(const MachineFunction &MF, 0
968 const SIProgramInfo &CurrentProgramInfo) { ----
969 const SIMachineFunctionInfo *MFI = MF.getInfo(); 0
970 const GCNSubtarget &STM = MF.getSubtarget(); 0
971 unsigned RsrcReg = getRsrcReg(MF.getFunction().getCallingConv()); 0
972 ----
973 if (AMDGPU::isCompute(MF.getFunction().getCallingConv())) { 0
974 OutStreamer->emitInt32(R_00B848_COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC1); 0
975 ----
976 OutStreamer->emitInt32(CurrentProgramInfo.getComputePGMRSrc1()); 0
977 ----
978 OutStreamer->emitInt32(R_00B84C_COMPUTE_PGM_RSRC2); 0
979 OutStreamer->emitInt32(CurrentProgramInfo.getComputePGMRSrc2()); 0
980 ----
981 OutStreamer->emitInt32(R_00B860_COMPUTE_TMPRING_SIZE); 0
982 OutStreamer->emitInt32( 0
983 STM.getGeneration() >= AMDGPUSubtarget::GFX11 0
984 ? S_00B860_WAVESIZE_GFX11Plus(CurrentProgramInfo.ScratchBlocks) 0
985 : S_00B860_WAVESIZE_PreGFX11(CurrentProgramInfo.ScratchBlocks)); 0
986 ----
987 // TODO: Should probably note flat usage somewhere. SC emits a "FlatPtr32 = ----
988 // 0" comment but I don't see a corresponding field in the register spec. ----
989 } else { ----
990 OutStreamer->emitInt32(RsrcReg); 0
991 OutStreamer->emitIntValue(S_00B028_VGPRS(CurrentProgramInfo.VGPRBlocks) | 0
992 S_00B028_SGPRS(CurrentProgramInfo.SGPRBlocks), 4); 0
993 OutStreamer->emitInt32(R_0286E8_SPI_TMPRING_SIZE); 0
994 OutStreamer->emitInt32( 0
995 STM.getGeneration() >= AMDGPUSubtarget::GFX11 0
996 ? S_0286E8_WAVESIZE_GFX11Plus(CurrentProgramInfo.ScratchBlocks) 0
997 : S_0286E8_WAVESIZE_PreGFX11(CurrentProgramInfo.ScratchBlocks)); 0
998 } ----
999 ----
1000 if (MF.getFunction().getCallingConv() == CallingConv::AMDGPU_PS) { 0
1001 OutStreamer->emitInt32(R_00B02C_SPI_SHADER_PGM_RSRC2_PS); 0
1002 unsigned ExtraLDSSize = STM.getGeneration() >= AMDGPUSubtarget::GFX11 0
1003 ? divideCeil(CurrentProgramInfo.LDSBlocks, 2) 0
1004 : CurrentProgramInfo.LDSBlocks; 0
1005 OutStreamer->emitInt32(S_00B02C_EXTRA_LDS_SIZE(ExtraLDSSize)); 0
1006 OutStreamer->emitInt32(R_0286CC_SPI_PS_INPUT_ENA); 0
1007 OutStreamer->emitInt32(MFI->getPSInputEnable()); 0
1008 OutStreamer->emitInt32(R_0286D0_SPI_PS_INPUT_ADDR); 0
1009 OutStreamer->emitInt32(MFI->getPSInputAddr()); 0
1010 } ----
1011 ----
1012 OutStreamer->emitInt32(R_SPILLED_SGPRS); 0
1013 OutStreamer->emitInt32(MFI->getNumSpilledSGPRs()); 0
1014 OutStreamer->emitInt32(R_SPILLED_VGPRS); 0
1015 OutStreamer->emitInt32(MFI->getNumSpilledVGPRs()); 0
1016 } 0
1017 ----
1018 // This is the equivalent of EmitProgramInfoSI above, but for when the OS type ----
1019 // is AMDPAL. It stores each compute/SPI register setting and other PAL ----
1020 // metadata items into the PALMD::Metadata, combining with any provided by the ----
1021 // frontend as LLVM metadata. Once all functions are written, the PAL metadata ----
1022 // is then written as a single block in the .note section. ----
1023 void AMDGPUAsmPrinter::EmitPALMetadata(const MachineFunction &MF, 0
1024 const SIProgramInfo &CurrentProgramInfo) { ----
1025 const SIMachineFunctionInfo *MFI = MF.getInfo(); 0
1026 auto CC = MF.getFunction().getCallingConv(); 0
1027 auto MD = getTargetStreamer()->getPALMetadata(); 0
1028 ----
1029 MD->setEntryPoint(CC, MF.getFunction().getName()); 0
1030 MD->setNumUsedVgprs(CC, CurrentProgramInfo.NumVGPRsForWavesPerEU); 0
1031 ----
1032 // Only set AGPRs for supported devices ----
1033 const GCNSubtarget &STM = MF.getSubtarget(); 0
1034 if (STM.hasMAIInsts()) { 0
1035 MD->setNumUsedAgprs(CC, CurrentProgramInfo.NumAccVGPR); 0
1036 } ----
1037 ----
1038 MD->setNumUsedSgprs(CC, CurrentProgramInfo.NumSGPRsForWavesPerEU); 0
1039 if (MD->getPALMajorVersion() < 3) { 0
1040 MD->setRsrc1(CC, CurrentProgramInfo.getPGMRSrc1(CC)); 0
1041 if (AMDGPU::isCompute(CC)) { 0
1042 MD->setRsrc2(CC, CurrentProgramInfo.getComputePGMRSrc2()); 0
1043 } else { ----
1044 if (CurrentProgramInfo.ScratchBlocks > 0) 0

1208 const char *ExtraCode, raw_ostream &O) { ----
1209 // First try the generic code, which knows about modifiers like 'c' and 'n'. ----
1210 if (!AsmPrinter::PrintAsmOperand(MI, OpNo, ExtraCode, O)) 0

1222 } ----
1223 } ----
1224 ----
1225 // TODO: Should be able to support other operand types like globals. ----

1230 return false; 0

1239 } else { ----
1240 O << format("0x%" PRIx64, static_cast(Val)); 0
1241 } ----
1242 return false; 0
1243 } ----
